========
1. 1. Preheat oven to 180 C / Gas 4.
2. 2. Place bacon in a large , deep frying pan.
3. 3. Cook over medium high heat until evenly brown.
4. 4. Drain , crumble and set aside.
5. 5. In a large pot with boiling salted water , cook pasta until al dente.
6. 6. Drain.
7. 7. In a medium frying pan , saute the chopped onion and garlic.
8. 8. Take off heat and add chopped cooked bacon and set aside.
9. 9. To make the sauce , in a medium saucepan melt the butter over low heat.
10. 10. Once melted , add the flour and stir constantly for 2 minutes.
11. 11. Gradually add milk and continue stirring until thickened.
12. 12. Stir in 2/3 of the grated Cheddar cheese and stir until melted.
13. 13. Combine cooked pasta , sauteed vegetables and sauce.
14. 14. Pour into a 2 litre baking dish.
15. 15. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 16. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 17. Serve warm.

16. 14. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 15. Serve warm.
7. 16. In a medium frying pan , saute the chopped onion and garlic.
8. 17. Take off heat and add chopped cooked bacon and set aside.

12. 17. Stir in 2/3 of the grated Cheddar cheese and stir until melted.

4. 8. Drain , crumble and set aside.
13. 9. Combine cooked pasta , sauteed vegetables and sauce.
14. 10. Pour into a 2 litre baking dish.
15. 11. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 12. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 13. Serve warm.
9. 14. To make the sauce , in a medium saucepan melt the butter over low heat.
10. 15. Once melted , add the flour and stir constantly for 2 minutes.
11. 16. Gradually add milk and continue stirring until thickened.
12. 17. Stir in 2/3 of the grated Cheddar cheese and stir until melted.

12. 9. Stir in 2/3 of the grated Cheddar cheese and stir until melted.

1. 1. Preheat oven to 180 C / Gas 4.
9. 2. To make the sauce , in a medium saucepan melt the butter over low heat.
10. 3. Once melted , add the flour and stir constantly for 2 minutes.
11. 4. Gradually add milk and continue stirring until thickened.
12. 5. Stir in 2/3 of the grated Cheddar cheese and stir until melted.
5. 6. In a large pot with boiling salted water , cook pasta until al dente.
6. 7. Drain.
13. 8. Combine cooked pasta , sauteed vegetables and sauce.
14. 9. Pour into a 2 litre baking dish.
15. 10. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 11. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 12. Serve warm.
7. 13. In a medium frying pan , saute the chopped onion and garlic.
8. 14. Take off heat and add chopped cooked bacon and set aside.
2. 15. Place bacon in a large , deep frying pan.
3. 16. Cook over medium high heat until evenly brown.
4. 17. Drain , crumble and set aside.

4. 13. Drain , crumble and set aside.
9. 14. To make the sauce , in a medium saucepan melt the butter over low heat.
10. 15. Once melted , add the flour and stir constantly for 2 minutes.
11. 16. Gradually add milk and continue stirring until thickened.
12. 17. Stir in 2/3 of the grated Cheddar cheese and stir until melted.
========

13. 2. Combine cooked pasta , sauteed vegetables and sauce.
14. 3. Pour into a 2 litre baking dish.
15. 4. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 5. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 6. Serve warm.
7. 7. In a medium frying pan , saute the chopped onion and garlic.
8. 8. Take off heat and add chopped cooked bacon and set aside.

6. 10. Drain.

15. 7. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 8. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 9. Serve warm.
5. 10. In a large pot with boiling salted water , cook pasta until al dente.
6. 11. Drain.
7. 12. In a medium frying pan , saute the chopped onion and garlic.
8. 13. Take off heat and add chopped cooked bacon and set aside.
9. 14. To make the sauce , in a medium saucepan melt the butter over low heat.
10. 15. Once melted , add the flour and stir constantly for 2 minutes.
11. 16. Gradually add milk and continue stirring until thickened.
12. 17. Stir in 2/3 of the grated Cheddar cheese and stir until melted.

1. 17. Preheat oven to 180 C / Gas 4.
========
2. 1. Place bacon in a large , deep frying pan.
3. 2. Cook over medium high heat until evenly brown.
4. 3. Drain , crumble and set aside.
5. 4. In a large pot with boiling salted water , cook pasta until al dente.
6. 5. Drain.
13. 6. Combine cooked pasta , sauteed vegetables and sauce.
14. 7. Pour into a 2 litre baking dish.
15. 8. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 9. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 10. Serve warm.
9. 11. To make the sauce , in a medium saucepan melt the butter over low heat.
10. 12. Once melted , add the flour and stir constantly for 2 minutes.
11. 13. Gradually add milk and continue stirring until thickened.
12. 14. Stir in 2/3 of the grated Cheddar cheese and stir until melted.

7. 16. In a medium frying pan , saute the chopped onion and garlic.
8. 17. Take off heat and add chopped cooked bacon and set aside.

6. 10. Drain.
13. 11. Combine cooked pasta , sauteed vegetables and sauce.
14. 12. Pour into a 2 litre baking dish.
15. 13. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 14. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 15. Serve warm.
7. 16. In a medium frying pan , saute the chopped onion and garlic.
8. 17. Take off heat and add chopped cooked bacon and set aside.
========
2. 1. Place bacon in a large , deep frying pan.
3. 2. Cook over medium high heat until evenly brown.
4. 3. Drain , crumble and set aside.
9. 4. To make the sauce , in a medium saucepan melt the butter over low heat.
10. 5. Once melted , add the flour and stir constantly for 2 minutes.
11. 6. Gradually add milk and continue stirring until thickened.
12. 7. Stir in 2/3 of the grated Cheddar cheese and stir until melted.
1. 8. Preheat oven to 180 C / Gas 4.
7. 9. In a medium frying pan , saute the chopped onion and garlic.
8. 10. Take off heat and add chopped cooked bacon and set aside.
5. 11. In a large pot with boiling salted water , cook pasta until al dente.
6. 12. Drain.
13. 13. Combine cooked pasta , sauteed vegetables and sauce.
14. 14. Pour into a 2 litre baking dish.
15. 15. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 16. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 17. Serve warm.

13. 4. Combine cooked pasta , sauteed vegetables and sauce.
14. 5. Pour into a 2 litre baking dish.
15. 6. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 7. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 8. Serve warm.
1. 9. Preheat oven to 180 C / Gas 4.
9. 10. To make the sauce , in a medium saucepan melt the butter over low heat.
10. 11. Once melted , add the flour and stir constantly for 2 minutes.
11. 12. Gradually add milk and continue stirring until thickened.
12. 13. Stir in 2/3 of the grated Cheddar cheese and stir until melted.
7. 14. In a medium frying pan , saute the chopped onion and garlic.
8. 15. Take off heat and add chopped cooked bacon and set aside.
5. 16. In a large pot with boiling salted water , cook pasta until al dente.
6. 17. Drain.

14. 14. Pour into a 2 litre baking dish.
15. 15. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 16. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 17. Serve warm.
========
5. 1. In a large pot with boiling salted water , cook pasta until al dente.
6. 2. Drain.
1. 3. Preheat oven to 180 C / Gas 4.
7. 4. In a medium frying pan , saute the chopped onion and garlic.
8. 5. Take off heat and add chopped cooked bacon and set aside.
9. 6. To make the sauce , in a medium saucepan melt the butter over low heat.
10. 7. Once melted , add the flour and stir constantly for 2 minutes.
11. 8. Gradually add milk and continue stirring until thickened.
12. 9. Stir in 2/3 of the grated Cheddar cheese and stir until melted.
13. 10. Combine cooked pasta , sauteed vegetables and sauce.
14. 11. Pour into a 2 litre baking dish.
15. 12. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 13. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 14. Serve warm.
2. 15. Place bacon in a large , deep frying pan.
3. 16. Cook over medium high heat until evenly brown.
4. 17. Drain , crumble and set aside.

9. 6. To make the sauce , in a medium saucepan melt the butter over low heat.
10. 7. Once melted , add the flour and stir constantly for 2 minutes.
11. 8. Gradually add milk and continue stirring until thickened.
12. 9. Stir in 2/3 of the grated Cheddar cheese and stir until melted.
1. 10. Preheat oven to 180 C / Gas 4.
7. 11. In a medium frying pan , saute the chopped onion and garlic.
8. 12. Take off heat and add chopped cooked bacon and set aside.
13. 13. Combine cooked pasta , sauteed vegetables and sauce.
14. 14. Pour into a 2 litre baking dish.
15. 15. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 16. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 17. Serve warm.
========

5. 1. In a large pot with boiling salted water , cook pasta until al dente.
6. 2. Drain.
7. 3. In a medium frying pan , saute the chopped onion and garlic.
8. 4. Take off heat and add chopped cooked bacon and set aside.
9. 5. To make the sauce , in a medium saucepan melt the butter over low heat.
10. 6. Once melted , add the flour and stir constantly for 2 minutes.
11. 7. Gradually add milk and continue stirring until thickened.
12. 8. Stir in 2/3 of the grated Cheddar cheese and stir until melted.
13. 9. Combine cooked pasta , sauteed vegetables and sauce.
14. 10. Pour into a 2 litre baking dish.
15. 11. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 12. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 13. Serve warm.
1. 14. Preheat oven to 180 C / Gas 4.
2. 15. Place bacon in a large , deep frying pan.
3. 16. Cook over medium high heat until evenly brown.
4. 17. Drain , crumble and set aside.

1. 12. Preheat oven to 180 C / Gas 4.
7. 13. In a medium frying pan , saute the chopped onion and garlic.
8. 14. Take off heat and add chopped cooked bacon and set aside.
2. 15. Place bacon in a large , deep frying pan.
3. 16. Cook over medium high heat until evenly brown.
4. 17. Drain , crumble and set aside.
========
5. 1. In a large pot with boiling salted water , cook pasta until al dente.
6. 2. Drain.
9. 3. To make the sauce , in a medium saucepan melt the butter over low heat.
10. 4. Once melted , add the flour and stir constantly for 2 minutes.
11. 5. Gradually add milk and continue stirring until thickened.
12. 6. Stir in 2/3 of the grated Cheddar cheese and stir until melted.
13. 7. Combine cooked pasta , sauteed vegetables and sauce.
14. 8. Pour into a 2 litre baking dish.
15. 9. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 10. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 11. Serve warm.

16. 6. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 7. Serve warm.
9. 8. To make the sauce , in a medium saucepan melt the butter over low heat.
10. 9. Once melted , add the flour and stir constantly for 2 minutes.
11. 10. Gradually add milk and continue stirring until thickened.
12. 11. Stir in 2/3 of the grated Cheddar cheese and stir until melted.
7. 12. In a medium frying pan , saute the chopped onion and garlic.
8. 13. Take off heat and add chopped cooked bacon and set aside.
2. 14. Place bacon in a large , deep frying pan.
3. 15. Cook over medium high heat until evenly brown.
4. 16. Drain , crumble and set aside.
1. 17. Preheat oven to 180 C / Gas 4.

16. 16. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 17. Serve warm.

7. 1. In a medium frying pan , saute the chopped onion and garlic.
8. 2. Take off heat and add chopped cooked bacon and set aside.
2. 3. Place bacon in a large , deep frying pan.
3. 4. Cook over medium high heat until evenly brown.
4. 5. Drain , crumble and set aside.
1. 6. Preheat oven to 180 C / Gas 4.
9. 7. To make the sauce , in a medium saucepan melt the butter over low heat.
10. 8. Once melted , add the flour and stir constantly for 2 minutes.
11. 9. Gradually add milk and continue stirring until thickened.
12. 10. Stir in 2/3 of the grated Cheddar cheese and stir until melted.
13. 11. Combine cooked pasta , sauteed vegetables and sauce.
14. 12. Pour into a 2 litre baking dish.
15. 13. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 14. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 15. Serve warm.
5. 16. In a large pot with boiling salted water , cook pasta until al dente.
6. 17. Drain.

1. 8. Preheat oven to 180 C / Gas 4.
9. 9. To make the sauce , in a medium saucepan melt the butter over low heat.
10. 10. Once melted , add the flour and stir constantly for 2 minutes.
11. 11. Gradually add milk and continue stirring until thickened.
12. 12. Stir in 2/3 of the grated Cheddar cheese and stir until melted.
13. 13. Combine cooked pasta , sauteed vegetables and sauce.
14. 14. Pour into a 2 litre baking dish.
15. 15. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 16. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 17. Serve warm.
========
7. 1. In a medium frying pan , saute the chopped onion and garlic.
8. 2. Take off heat and add chopped cooked bacon and set aside.
5. 3. In a large pot with boiling salted water , cook pasta until al dente.
6. 4. Drain.
2. 5. Place bacon in a large , deep frying pan.
3. 6. Cook over medium high heat until evenly brown.
4. 7. Drain , crumble and set aside.

9. 3. To make the sauce , in a medium saucepan melt the butter over low heat.
10. 4. Once melted , add the flour and stir constantly for 2 minutes.
11. 5. Gradually add milk and continue stirring until thickened.
12. 6. Stir in 2/3 of the grated Cheddar cheese and stir until melted.
2. 7. Place bacon in a large , deep frying pan.
3. 8. Cook over medium high heat until evenly brown.
4. 9. Drain , crumble and set aside.
13. 10. Combine cooked pasta , sauteed vegetables and sauce.
14. 11. Pour into a 2 litre baking dish.
15. 12. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 13. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 14. Serve warm.
1. 15. Preheat oven to 180 C / Gas 4.
5. 16. In a large pot with boiling salted water , cook pasta until al dente.
6. 17. Drain.

12. 14. Stir in 2/3 of the grated Cheddar cheese and stir until melted.
2. 15. Place bacon in a large , deep frying pan.
3. 16. Cook over medium high heat until evenly brown.
4. 17. Drain , crumble and set aside.
========
7. 1. In a medium frying pan , saute the chopped onion and garlic.
8. 2. Take off heat and add chopped cooked bacon and set aside.
13. 3. Combine cooked pasta , sauteed vegetables and sauce.
14. 4. Pour into a 2 litre baking dish.
15. 5. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 6. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 7. Serve warm.

8. 7. Take off heat and add chopped cooked bacon and set aside.
13. 8. Combine cooked pasta , sauteed vegetables and sauce.
14. 9. Pour into a 2 litre baking dish.
15. 10. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 11. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 12. Serve warm.
5. 13. In a large pot with boiling salted water , cook pasta until al dente.
6. 14. Drain.
2. 15. Place bacon in a large , deep frying pan.
3. 16. Cook over medium high heat until evenly brown.
4. 17. Drain , crumble and set aside.
========
9. 1. To make the sauce , in a medium saucepan melt the butter over low heat.
10. 2. Once melted , add the flour and stir constantly for 2 minutes.
11. 3. Gradually add milk and continue stirring until thickened.
12. 4. Stir in 2/3 of the grated Cheddar cheese and stir until melted.
1. 5. Preheat oven to 180 C / Gas 4.
13. 6. Combine cooked pasta , sauteed vegetables and sauce.
14. 7. Pour into a 2 litre baking dish.
15. 8. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 9. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 10. Serve warm.
2. 11. Place bacon in a large , deep frying pan.
3. 12. Cook over medium high heat until evenly brown.
4. 13. Drain , crumble and set aside.
5. 14. In a large pot with boiling salted water , cook pasta until al dente.
6. 15. Drain.
7. 16. In a medium frying pan , saute the chopped onion and garlic.
8. 17. Take off heat and add chopped cooked bacon and set aside.

9. 1. To make the sauce , in a medium saucepan melt the butter over low heat.
10. 2. Once melted , add the flour and stir constantly for 2 minutes.
11. 3. Gradually add milk and continue stirring until thickened.
12. 4. Stir in 2/3 of the grated Cheddar cheese and stir until melted.
2. 5. Place bacon in a large , deep frying pan.
3. 6. Cook over medium high heat until evenly brown.
4. 7. Drain , crumble and set aside.
13. 8. Combine cooked pasta , sauteed vegetables and sauce.
14. 9. Pour into a 2 litre baking dish.
15. 10. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 11. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 12. Serve warm.
5. 13. In a large pot with boiling salted water , cook pasta until al dente.
6. 14. Drain.
7. 15. In a medium frying pan , saute the chopped onion and garlic.
8. 16. Take off heat and add chopped cooked bacon and set aside.

6. 12. Drain.
13. 13. Combine cooked pasta , sauteed vegetables and sauce.
14. 14. Pour into a 2 litre baking dish.
15. 15. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 16. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 17. Serve warm.
========
9. 1. To make the sauce , in a medium saucepan melt the butter over low heat.
10. 2. Once melted , add the flour and stir constantly for 2 minutes.
11. 3. Gradually add milk and continue stirring until thickened.
12. 4. Stir in 2/3 of the grated Cheddar cheese and stir until melted.
7. 5. In a medium frying pan , saute the chopped onion and garlic.
8. 6. Take off heat and add chopped cooked bacon and set aside.
1. 7. Preheat oven to 180 C / Gas 4.
2. 8. Place bacon in a large , deep frying pan.
3. 9. Cook over medium high heat until evenly brown.
4. 10. Drain , crumble and set aside.
13. 11. Combine cooked pasta , sauteed vegetables and sauce.
14. 12. Pour into a 2 litre baking dish.
15. 13. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 14. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 15. Serve warm.

6. 17. Drain.

13. 5. Combine cooked pasta , sauteed vegetables and sauce.
14. 6. Pour into a 2 litre baking dish.
15. 7. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 8. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 9. Serve warm.
1. 10. Preheat oven to 180 C / Gas 4.
7. 11. In a medium frying pan , saute the chopped onion and garlic.
8. 12. Take off heat and add chopped cooked bacon and set aside.
2. 13. Place bacon in a large , deep frying pan.
3. 14. Cook over medium high heat until evenly brown.
4. 15. Drain , crumble and set aside.
5. 16. In a large pot with boiling salted water , cook pasta until al dente.
6. 17. Drain.

7. 16. In a medium frying pan , saute the chopped onion and garlic.
8. 17. Take off heat and add chopped cooked bacon and set aside.
========
13. 1. Combine cooked pasta , sauteed vegetables and sauce.
14. 2. Pour into a 2 litre baking dish.
15. 3. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 4. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 5. Serve warm.

5. 9. In a large pot with boiling salted water , cook pasta until al dente.
6. 10. Drain.
9. 11. To make the sauce , in a medium saucepan melt the butter over low heat.
10. 12. Once melted , add the flour and stir constantly for 2 minutes.
11. 13. Gradually add milk and continue stirring until thickened.
12. 14. Stir in 2/3 of the grated Cheddar cheese and stir until melted.
7. 15. In a medium frying pan , saute the chopped onion and garlic.
8. 16. Take off heat and add chopped cooked bacon and set aside.
1. 17. Preheat oven to 180 C / Gas 4.
========
13. 1. Combine cooked pasta , sauteed vegetables and sauce.
14. 2. Pour into a 2 litre baking dish.
15. 3. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 4. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 5. Serve warm.

13. 1. Combine cooked pasta , sauteed vegetables and sauce.
14. 2. Pour into a 2 litre baking dish.
15. 3. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 4. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 5. Serve warm.
5. 6. In a large pot with boiling salted water , cook pasta until al dente.
6. 7. Drain.
7. 8. In a medium frying pan , saute the chopped onion and garlic.
8. 9. Take off heat and add chopped cooked bacon and set aside.
2. 10. Place bacon in a large , deep frying pan.
3. 11. Cook over medium high heat until evenly brown.
4. 12. Drain , crumble and set aside.
9. 13. To make the sauce , in a medium saucepan melt the butter over low heat.
10. 14. Once melted , add the flour and stir constantly for 2 minutes.
11. 15. Gradually add milk and continue stirring until thickened.
12. 16. Stir in 2/3 of the grated Cheddar cheese and stir until melted.
1. 17. Preheat oven to 180 C / Gas 4.
========

2. 13. Place bacon in a large , deep frying pan.
3. 14. Cook over medium high heat until evenly brown.
4. 15. Drain , crumble and set aside.
5. 16. In a large pot with boiling salted water , cook pasta until al dente.
6. 17. Drain.
========
13. 1. Combine cooked pasta , sauteed vegetables and sauce.
14. 2. Pour into a 2 litre baking dish.
15. 3. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 4. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 5. Serve warm.
7. 6. In a medium frying pan , saute the chopped onion and garlic.
8. 7. Take off heat and add chopped cooked bacon and set aside.
9. 8. To make the sauce , in a medium saucepan melt the butter over low heat.
10. 9. Once melted , add the flour and stir constantly for 2 minutes.
11. 10. Gradually add milk and continue stirring until thickened.
12. 11. Stir in 2/3 of the grated Cheddar cheese and stir until melted.
1. 12. Preheat oven to 180 C / Gas 4.

10. 7. Once melted , add the flour and stir constantly for 2 minutes.
11. 8. Gradually add milk and continue stirring until thickened.
12. 9. Stir in 2/3 of the grated Cheddar cheese and stir until melted.
7. 10. In a medium frying pan , saute the chopped onion and garlic.
8. 11. Take off heat and add chopped cooked bacon and set aside.
5. 12. In a large pot with boiling salted water , cook pasta until al dente.
6. 13. Drain.
1. 14. Preheat oven to 180 C / Gas 4.
2. 15. Place bacon in a large , deep frying pan.
3. 16. Cook over medium high heat until evenly brown.
4. 17. Drain , crumble and set aside.

13. 1. Combine cooked pasta , sauteed vegetables and sauce.
14. 2. Pour into a 2 litre baking dish.
15. 3. Sprinkle over remaining Cheddar cheese.
16. 4. Bake uncovered in preheated oven until cheese on top is melted and brown , 15 to 20 minutes.
17. 5. Serve warm.
